    1                                                module ucie_sb_tx_path (
    2                                                
    3                                                    input logic i_clk,    // System / Control Clock
    4                                                    input logic i_s_clk,  // SerDes Clock  — pattern generation & output
    5                                                    input logic i_reset,  // Active-high asynchronous reset
    6                                                
    7                                                    // Control inputs
    8                                                    input logic i_sb_init_start,  // High during sideband initialisation
    9                                                    input logic i_timer_1ms,      // Pulse every 1 ms (from Timer module)
    10                                                   input logic i_rx_done,        // From RX path — pattern detected
    11                                               
    12                                                   // Physical outputs  (registered on i_s_clk)
    13                                                   output logic o_tx_sb_data,
    14                                                   output logic o_tx_sb_clk,
    15                                               
    16                                                   // Control output  (combinational from i_clk domain
    17                                                   output logic o_stop  // High when initialisation is fully done
    18                                               
    19                                               );
    20                                               
    21                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------
    22                                                 // Internal States & Counters
    23                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------
    24                                                 localparam IDLE = 2'b00;
    25                                                 localparam CYCLING = 2'b01;  // Alternating 1ms ON / 1ms OFF
    26                                                 localparam EXTRA_ITERS = 2'b10;  // Sending final 4 iterations
    27                                                 localparam DONE = 2'b11;  // Initialization complete
    28                                               
    29                                                 logic [1:0] current_state, next_state, current_state_serdes;
    30                                               
    31                                                 // Pattern Counters
    32                                                 // Total pattern length = 64 UI (Clk) + 32 UI (Low) = 96 UI
    33                                                 logic [6:0] ui_counter;  // Counter 0 to 95
    34                                                 logic [2:0] iter_counter;  // Counter 0 to 4 (for the extra iterations)
    35                                               
    36                                                 // 1ms Toggle Logic
    37                                                 logic       r_1ms_active;  // 1: Generating, 0: Quiet (swaps every 1ms)
    38                                                 logic       r_1ms_active_serdes;
    39                                               
    40                                                 // Generated Signals
    41                                                 logic       w_gen_data;
    42                                                 logic       w_gen_clk;
    43                                                 logic       w_pattern_running;  // High when we are actually shifting bits out
    44                                               
    45                                                 logic       r_clk_en_safe;
    46                                               
    47                                                 // Used to account for the time differences btw the slow clock and fast clock 
    48                                                 // since when detection is done and ui_counter reaches 95 and rx_done is asserted 
    49                                                 // we should go to Extra Iter state but we need to wait for the slow clock edge to come
    50                                                 // and between that the ui counter might move to 0 again to start next iterations before 
    51                                                 // the slow clock edge come --- That is why we need a flag to remeber this scene
    52                                                 logic       latch_flag;
    53                                               
    54                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------
    55                                                 // 1ms Alternating Logic
    56                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------
    57              1                       2718       always_ff @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin
    58                                                   if (i_reset) begin
    59              1                        262           r_1ms_active <= 1'b1;  // Start active
    60                                                   end else if (current_state == IDLE) begin
    61              1                       1466           r_1ms_active <= 1'b1;
    62                                                   end else if (i_timer_1ms && (current_state == CYCLING || current_state == EXTRA_ITERS)) begin
    63              1                        321           r_1ms_active <= ~r_1ms_active;  // Toggle every 1ms
    64                                                   end
    65                                                 end
    66

    68                                                 // Main FSM
    69                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    297             1                      77273           stall_flag      <= 1'b1; // Mark that first message has been processed
    298                                                  end
    299                                                  else if (stall_flag)begin
    300             1                      38547           o_req           <= o_req;
    301             1                      38547           o_resp          <= o_resp;
    302             1                      38547           o_info_out      <= o_info_out;
    303             1                      38547           o_data_out      <= o_data_out;
    304             1                      38547           o_decoding      <= o_decoding;
    305             1                      38547           o_valid         <= o_valid;
    306                                                  end
    307                                                  else begin
    308             1                      76597           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    309             1                      76597           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    310             1                      76597           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    293                                              
    294                                                //---- SEQUENTIAL PROCESSES --------------------------------------------------
    295                                                //Decoding process
    296             1                     347791       always @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin
    297                                                  if (i_reset) begin
    298             1                        236           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    299             1                        236           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    300             1                        236           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    301             1                        236           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    302             1                        236           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    303             1                        236           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    304             1                        236           stall_flag      <= 1'b0;
    305                                                  end
    306                                                  else begin
    307                                                  if (i_done || invalid_dec) begin
    308             1                     146135           stall_flag      <= 1'b0; // Clear stall flag on done signal
    309             1                     146135           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    310             1                     146135           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    311             1                     146135           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    312             1                     146135           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    313             1                     146135           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    314             1                     146135           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    315                                                  end
    316                                              
    317                                                  else if (!i_empty && !stall_flag) begin
    318             1                      80267           o_valid         <= dec_valid; // Valid message
    319             1                      80267           o_info_out      <= o_info_out_w; // Extract info field from input message
    320             1                      80267           o_data_out      <= o_data_out_w; // Extract data field from input message
    321             1                      80267           o_req           <= dec_req;
    322             1                      80267           o_resp          <= dec_resp;
    323             1                      80267           o_decoding      <= dec_decoding;
    324             1                      80267           stall_flag      <= 1'b1; // Mark that first message has been processed
    325                                                  end
    326                                                  else if (stall_flag)begin
    327             1                      41154           o_req           <= o_req;
    328             1                      41154           o_resp          <= o_resp;
    329             1                      41154           o_info_out      <= o_info_out;
    330             1                      41154           o_data_out      <= o_data_out;
    331             1                      41154           o_decoding      <= o_decoding;
    332             1                      41154           o_valid         <= o_valid;
    333                                                  end
    334                                                  else begin
    335             1                      79999           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    336             1                      79999           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    337             1                      79999           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    338             1                      79999           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    339             1                      79999           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    340             1                      79999           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    341                                                  end
    342                                                  end
    343                                                end // Decoding_proc
    344                                              
    345                                              
    346                                                //---- COMBINATIONAL LOGIC ---------------------------------------------------
    347                                              // --- Combinational parity and field extraction ---
    348                                              assign dec_msg_code    = i_msg_in[117:110];
    349                                              assign dec_msg_subcode = i_msg_in[71:64];
    350                                              assign dec_op_code     = i_msg_in[100:96];
    351                                              assign dec_srcid       = i_msg_in[127:125];
    352                                              assign dec_dstid       = i_msg_in[90:88];
    353             1                      50714     assign dec_dp          = ^{i_msg_in[63:0]};
    354             1                     207714     assign dec_cp          = ^{{i_msg_in[127:96], i_msg_in[93:64]}};
    355                                              
    356             1                     314190     assign dec_valid       = (invalid_dec) ? 1'b0 : ((dec_cp == i_msg_in[94]) && (dec_dp == i_msg_in[95]));
    357                                              
    358             1                     368276     assign o_dec_ready = !i_empty && !stall_flag;
    359             1                     283539     assign o_info_out_w =  (invalid_dec) ? {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[87:72];
    360             1                     134138     assign o_data_out_w = (invalid_dec) ? {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[63:0];
